<script type="text/javascript">
    var _expandedGroupId = '49';
    var matchId = '14908632';
    $(document).ready(function () {

        $(this).scrollTop(0);

        SubscribeToMatch('14908632');

        //$(".odd-type-group-header-menu.slick-initialized").slick('unslick');
        //$(".odd-type-group-header-menu").slick({
        //    dots: false,
        //    infinite: false,
        //    speed: 300,
        //    slidesToShow: 3,
        //    slidesToScroll: 'auto',
        //    centerMode: false,
        //    variableWidth: true,
        //    swipeToSlide: true,
        //    autoplay: false,
        //    arrows: false,
        //});

        /* -------- set height of LMT iframe ------- */
        var eventMethod = window.addEventListener
            ? "addEventListener"
            : "attachEvent";
        var eventer = window[eventMethod];
        var messageEvent = eventMethod === "attachEvent"
            ? "onmessage"
            : "message";

        eventer(messageEvent, function (e) {
            if (!isEmpty(e.origin == "https://1.bahisbilir.com") && e.type == 'message' && e.isTrusted) {
                if (e.data > 50) {
                    var iframe_height = e.data;
                    $("#LiveTrackerIframe").css('height', iframe_height + 'px');
                }
            }
        });
        /* -------- ------- */

        $(".live_match_detail_page .match-odd").off('click').on('click', function () {
            var liveMatchId = $(this).attr("data-matchid");
            var liveMatchOddId = $(this).attr("data-matchoddid");
            var liveMatchOddValueType = $(this).attr("data-matchoddvaluetype");
            processLiveMatchOdd(liveMatchId, liveMatchOddId, liveMatchOddValueType);
        });

        $("#goback").click(function () {
            liveMatchList();
        });
        processMatchStatusDetails('14908632');

        updateActiveBetItems();
        MatchOddsInitialHideRows();

        if (LIVE_STREAM_AUTO_OPEN)
            PlayLiveStreammarmaraBet('', 'Botafogo RJ'+' - '+'Ceara-ce');

        //expand or collapse grupe marketa
        $(".live_match_data[data-matchid='{0}'] div.odd_type_group_header".format(matchId)).click(function () {

            var odd_type_group_body = $(this).next("div.odd_type_group_body");
            var alreadyShown = odd_type_group_body.hasClass("shown");

            if (!alreadyShown) {
                $(this).addClass('shown-header');
                odd_type_group_body.addClass("shown");
            } else {
                $(this).removeClass('shown-header');
                odd_type_group_body.removeClass("shown");
            }
        });

        // izbor grupe iz group menija
        $(".live_match_data[data-matchid='{0}'] .odd-type-group-header-menu span".format(matchId)).click(function () {

            $(".live_match_data[data-matchid='{0}'] .odd-type-group-header-menu span".format(matchId)).removeClass("selected");
            $(this).addClass('selected');

            var selectedGroupId = $(this).attr("data-groupid");
            if (selectedGroupId == -1) {
                $(".live_match_data[data-matchid='{0}'] div.odd_type_group".format(matchId)).removeClass("not-visible");
                $(".live_match_data[data-matchid='{0}'] div.odd_type_group_header".format(matchId)).addClass('shown-header');
                $(".live_match_data[data-matchid='{0}'] div.odd_type_group_body".format(matchId)).addClass('shown');
            } else {
                $(".live_match_data[data-matchid='{0}'] div.odd_type_group".format(matchId)).addClass("not-visible");
                $(".live_match_data[data-matchid='{0}'] div.odd_type_group[data-groupid='{1}']".format(matchId, selectedGroupId)).removeClass("not-visible");

                $(".live_match_data[data-matchid='{0}'] div.odd_type_group .odd_type_group_header.shown-header".format(matchId)).removeClass('shown-header');
                $(".live_match_data[data-matchid='{0}'] div.odd_type_group[data-groupid='{1}'] .odd_type_group_header".format(matchId, selectedGroupId)).addClass('shown-header');

                $(".live_match_data[data-matchid='{0}'] div.odd_type_group .odd_type_group_body.shown".format(matchId)).removeClass('shown');
                $(".live_match_data[data-matchid='{0}'] div.odd_type_group[data-groupid='{1}'] .odd_type_group_body".format(matchId, selectedGroupId)).addClass('shown');
            }
        });

        $(".live_match_data[data-matchid='{0}'] .odd-type-group-header-menu span[data-groupid='{1}']".format(matchId, -1)).click();
        if (_expandedGroupId > 0) {
            $(".live_match_data[data-matchid='{0}'] div.odd_type_group .odd_type_group_header.shown-header".format(matchId)).removeClass('shown-header');
            $(".live_match_data[data-matchid='{0}'] div.odd_type_group[data-groupid='{1}'] .odd_type_group_header".format(matchId, _expandedGroupId)).addClass('shown-header');

            $(".live_match_data[data-matchid='{0}'] div.odd_type_group .odd_type_group_body.shown".format(matchId)).removeClass('shown');
            $(".live_match_data[data-matchid='{0}'] div.odd_type_group[data-groupid='{1}'] .odd_type_group_body".format(matchId, _expandedGroupId)).addClass('shown');
        }

		STATSCOREWidgets.onLoad(err => {
			if (err) {
				switch (err.type) {
					case 'NetworkError':
						break;

					case 'BrowserNotSupported':
						break;
				}

				return;
			}

			const element = document.getElementById('myWidget');
            const configurationId = '65c592e745164675a446d35b';
			const inputData = { eventId: 'm:14908632', language: 'en' };
			const options = {loader: {enabled: true, color1: '#FA0A32', color2: '#191C18'}};

			const widget = new window.STATSCOREWidgets.WidgetGroup(element, configurationId, inputData, options);
		});

    });
</script>
